<Author>BlueRidgeBadger
<Content>Cute and convenient We spent two nights before a trip to eastern Puerto Rico and three nights after at this cute little hotel in Condado and had a very nice stay. There's nothing spectacular about the hotel, but it's quite pleasant and much more affordable than other comparable options.The rooms have nice marble floors, large whirlpool tubs, (small) flat screen tvs with cable, internet connections, ceiling fans, high-powered AC units, and the in-room minibars are wine fridges with enough space to add a few items of your own. The hotel also offers a better-than-average breakfast, a very small but cute pool, a rooftop jacuzzi, on-site laundry facilities (one coin-operated washer and dryer, $2 each), several very pleasant sitting areas, both inside and out, and friendly staff. The hotel is within a few blocks of a beach, lots of restaurants, a 24-hour Walgreens, a post office, a bus stop to Old San Juan (about a 10-minute ride), and several bigger hotel/resort/casinos, and is about 5 or 6 blocks from the Museo de Arte Contemporaneo de Puerto Rico.The rooms are small, but not uncomfortably so. The mattresses in the two rooms we stayed in were not uncomfortable at first, but their lack of firm support made them a bit hard on my back after a night or two. The bathtubs are lovely but there's no water pressure at all in the showers.So, if you're planning to explore San Juan, and particularly if you're more interested in exploring Old San Juan and Puerto Rican art, culture, history and cuisine than lying on pristine beaches, this hotel will meet all your needs nicely, conveniently, and affordably. If you want to spend a lot of time luxuriating in your room and in your hotel, this is not where you want to stay--there's no in-house restaurant or bar  hence no room service, and there's no view from your window. The beach that's a two-minute walk from the hotel is ok but it's not great: there's plenty of space for swimming, but it's lined with kind of low-to-mid-range hotels and resorts and abandoned, sometimes dilapidated, buildings. Playa Condado is not too far away, either--maybe a 10- or 15-minute walk west down Ashford Ave. It's nicer but sandwiched between a hotel and a very busy bridge; it also has lots of rocks and seaweed/sea grass and is very, very small. If beaches are your focus in San Juan, you'll be disappointed; if you'd just like to visit beaches occasionally amidst other activities, this cute, friendly hotel should suit you well.  
<Date>Dec 28, 2008

<Content>Would Definitely Stay Again! Our group (3 middle-aged couples) stayed here two nights pre-cruise in March (admittedly, this review is late!). We have to travel on a budget, and, after reading the Tripadvisor reviews, decided to give it a try. We were more than satisfied. The rooms were not fancy but clean. We loved the public areas. The continental breakfast was served in a lovely courtyard area--pretty and peaceful and a great way to gear up for your day. The rooftop terrace was perfect for winding down at night after a long day of sightseeing. The staff was very friendly and helpful. We did have some problems getting our reservations straightened out (in advance of our arrival) but the staff was extremely apologetic and finally fixed the problem. The location was convenient. Of course, we would have loved to have had a beachfront hotel with an ocean view, but for the price, we could not have asked for more. We are looking forward to going back.

<Author>BrnzBarbie22
<Content>Nice Room, Great Rate! After reading all the reviews on the Coral Princess, I was pleased to find this hotel delivers what most positive reviews had to say. Overall, it was a very charming hotel that will definitely stay on my short list of favorites in the San Juan area.I was traveling single and I stayed in room 19. It was one of the smaller rooms, but still very adequate. The room was very clean and room service was dependable. The ceiling fan worked great - so much that I could go without the air condition at night.Here are a few things I didn't see in other reviews that might be helpful. There is 24 hour security at the front desk, someone has to buzz you in at all times of the day. I felt very secure, but it was inconvenient one night about 3am when I had to wait about 5 minutes for the attendent to return to the desk.They have a very convenient room 11, where you can leave your bags before or after checkout. This room is also equiped with a bathroom and shower so you can get cleaned up before heading to the airport if you have a late flight.There is a refrigerator in each room, but it is fully stocked and the hotel charges very convenient prices for their refreshments. There was a Walgreens around the corner. I bought my own refreshements, but they still attempted to charge me for items from the wet bar at the end of my stay.The only complaint I had would be a general hotel gripe: the room door was not very soundproof and you can hear noise out in the hallway. There were a couple of times I was awakened by the child across the hall, but that did not take away from the overall experience.

<Author>WildCat75
<Content>A princess stay at the Coral Princess Inn!! Date May 27th 2008Reviewers: Mr.  Mrs. Zutter, Calgary, Alberta, CanadaWe stayed at the Coral Princess Inn for one night on May 17th, and we absolutely loved this little inn full of enchantment.We went to Puerto Rico, on a long awaited honeymoon, we got married on Oct of 2001 but due to a lot of different circumstances we were not able to go on a honeymoon trip.This year we were finally able to take the time and have the finances to do so, and we wanted this trip to be PERFECT. We booked a state room in the Carnival Destiny departing San Juan late on Sunday May 18th, and we decided that we would travel the Friday before so we would have 2 days in Puerto Rico, we had just taken our in classroom and pool Scuba course and we only needed to take the 4 Open Water Classes to finish our Certification and we wanted to do this in San Juan before the trip. I was looking for a small hotel that would offer great service and be personable, since my husband and I both like to experience the culture of the countries we travel to, and I have to say that Coral Princess Inn did not disappoint!!Here is what I mean by this, we arrived in San Juan at 8:30 AM that morning, the check in wasn't untill 2:00 PM, and we were going straight to La Casa Del Buzo to go on our first 2 Open water classes as soon as we arrived, for this matter and because we couldn't wait around for check in at 2:00 pm, the hotel let us put our luggage in a small room that had a shower and that could be locked so we wouldn鈥檛 have to worry about our stuff, they also let us use their phone as many times as we needed to call the Scuba store (the lad that took my call from Calgary had not booked us in for the classes and the owner of 鈥淟a Casa del Buzo鈥?very promptly found us an instructor to take my husband and I out for the dives) so we had to call back and forth to arrange this, we went off and did our first 2 dives and by the time we came back our room was ready and front desk had us checked in, in a couple of minutes, the room was very clean and comfortable we never had any problems with water pressure or anything, it is not a luxury hotel but we were static about our accommodations, all the employees were super friendly and helpful, and they were quick to give directions to places and help with anything we needed.The little hotel has a beautiful indoor patio, a little pool, as well as a Jacuzzi tub on the terrace, we didn鈥檛 get to use them but they looked clean and attractive under the heat of the day! The location of The Coral Princess Inn is also very convenient, the beach is a couple of blocks away which is a long golden strip bordered by beautiful hotels, and a sea as blue as the summer sky, there is also a 24 hour Walgreens half a block away were you can purchase from toiletries to water bottles, to anything you find you need in a hurry. There is also a lot of small stores including a Subway restaurant, photo stores, liquor stores, and much much more, just in the blocks around the hotel, take a walk and immerse yourself in the Puerto Rican culture of music, laughter and camaraderie.A short walk away there is a little restaurant called 鈥淟a Ropa Vieja鈥?that served us with impeccable curtsey and if you are a Risotto lover PLEASE try their Shrimp Risotto, Oh!! I have never tasted something as decadent!!! Both my husband and I had to meet the cook, as this was the best Risotto we ever tasted!!The next morning we had to check out at 11:00 am, and since we had to leave around 8:00 am to go do our last 2 Scuba classes, front desk let us check out early and let us keep our suitcases in the little room under lock again, we left for the whole day and didn鈥檛 worry about loosing our stuff or having to keep our huge luggage in the heat in our Scuba instructor鈥檚 car鈥?when we came back we were able to use the shower in that little room, change and get ready to board our Cruise ship!!All in all I LOVED this little hotel that is so conveniently located, and has helpful and friendly staff. We would definitely stay there again and we will recommend it without a problem! They made our 2 days in Puerto Rico the stay of a lifetime!! And the perfect start to our 7 day Southern Caribbean Cruise vacation!!

<Author>vvv3
<Content>Definitely recommend Stayed for 5 nights based on the good reviews on this site. Was one of the best deals in San Juan, even with the substantial taxes/fees added (which are listed in the confirmation email as a final price). The rooms were larger than I expected from what I had read. Small flat-screen TV with a bunch of channels for pre-bed dozing off. The pool is small but useful. The rooftop hot tub is hit or miss as it wasn't always working. Breakfast was basic (from Costco) but enough to get you going in the morning. The staff was very helpful and one maintenance issue that appeared was resolved immediately. It was possible to find parking always either in front of the hotel or on side streets so never had to pay extra. And the location is very convenient for Condado, which seems to be rapidly expanding. Lots of restaurants and shops around, including a very useful Walgreens one block away. Cab fare to downtown San Juan was $12 if you don't feel like driving (didn't try the bus). Overall, this hotel is a good value in a good location, so I would definitely recommend it for visitors to Puerto Rico.

<Author>Movintovieques
<Content>Coral Princess Inn We enjoyed our stay at The Coral Princess. It was our last hotel of the trip and overall it was a nice place, but I was expecting more. The hotel does add a lot of taxes and charges though, so be aware of that. It was almost the price of another night. The patios and balconys were wonderful. The room was nice, though a little dirtier than I expected, but still not bad. The bathroom was the worst part, but still very manageable. A little bit of mildew and it just looked older, like it should be retiled and regrouted. We were a little bored in this part of town though. Nightlife is pretty lacking if you don't feel like getting ripped off at the casinos and not really that many places to eat as far as variety goes. There is a huge Chili's down the street, but that just isn't a place we travel to Puerto Rico to eat at. The beaches are great though, we really enjoyed them.

<Author>graceCP
<Content>Excellent atmosphere at Coral Princess Our party of 6 stayed for 3 nights at the Coral Princess Inn,in early April.It is small and quaint but clean and in a good location.The staff were informative and competent.The rooms were clean but really tiny;our suitcases had to be pushed into corners between the bed and the wall ,but we overlooked that small inconvenience since there were so many positive things.While our room,(room 3) was tiny,(with a tiny window over the bed that looked out onto a corridor)one of the other couples had room 4,which was much bigger for the same rate.It had a window that looked outside.The couple that had room 8 near the breakfast area also ended up in cramped quarters,but like us,considered it a minor inconvenience.The breakfast(which was included with the cost of the room)was more than adequate for our needs and the casual atmosphere was lovely.We could make our own toast/bagels,tea/etc.,choose what we wanted(cheese slices,ham slices,pastries,yogurt,fruit,etc)and then sit in the courtyard while we ate,and listened to the birdsong.We absolutely loved it!The pool was very small but the beach was only a few minutes away;right across the road.On the third floor there is a hot tub that is open till 9 P.M. (though the staff allowed my friends and I to stay in until 11,which was considerate).The food at the nearby Cafe Angel(try the mofongo if you want a taste of the national dish)was excellent;reasonably priced and huge portions.Also the Black Angus Steakhouse serves the best steaks that you could ever ask for.There is a Walgreens around the corner.If you want to go to Old San Juan or the mall(The Plaza of the Americas)you don't need to waste your money on a cab;the B21 bus runs right near the inn and drops you off there as well(every 20 minutes).It costs just .75 cents each way.The exact change is required.Overall,I would certainly recommend this hotel to anyone who is budget conscious and just wants somewhere clean and homey to stay for a short time.It is no Hilton,but then you don't pay Hilton prices either. At 125.00 a night it's not bad,as rates go in San Juan.

<Author>gypsywmn
<Content>The value just wasn't there... I saw all of the good reviews on trip advisor for this hotel and started to search around for prices. I found them listed on hotels.com with a price of $115 per night, but no mention of the bed size, and we wanted a queen or bigger. I decided to contact the hotel directly and they offered me a queen bed at $135 a night, which seemed a little high, but I decided the extra $20 per night would be okay. Watch out for the additional fees, though. They charged an additional $9.00 per day as a maintenance fee or something like that, and there is a 14% tax on top of that. We ended up paying $682 for 4 nights, or $170 per night. Now, I was looking for a small, quaint hotel that would bring with it the charm of the local community, and a sense that we were experiencing a part of Puerto Rico. This hotel just didn't offer that. This was a $100 per night hotel at best. For $170 a night, we shouldn't have had the following problems: The first night there, the water would only turn on cold. There were 2 of us, and we turned the knobs every which way trying to get hot water in the shower. Finally, we asked at the desk. They agreed to look at it in the morning while we had breakfast. After, they brought us in, and showed us how to turn the knob and said the hot water was working all along. There is no way it was working prior to that. Why couldn't they just apologize for having to turn on the water heater? In addition, after breakfast, we brought our coffee back into the room with us while we were getting ready. When they cleaned the room, they didn't remove the empty, used coffee cups. For the price we were paying, I would expect the room to be perfect when we returned for the evening. I ended up having to bring 2 days of coffee cups back out to the breakfast area myself. I know these things seem small, and I would overlook them for a less expensive hotel, but I know there are other hotels in the area that provide better service for the same price. (I had previously stayed at the Wind Chimes Inn and would have booked there again, if they weren't all filled up.) The good things: the courtyard for breakfast was beautiful, but don't expect anything very healthy (yogurt with lots of sugar, pastries, and processed cheese and ham... they also had cereal, but only cornflakes.) The bed was the right size, but it was just outside the courtyard, so when people would congregate for breakfast, they woke us up every morning. No need to set an alarm! The rooms were cleaned well except for the coffee cup issue, and the location was great.If you are going to stay here, I would ask NOT to have a room near the courtyard, and be careful about pricing. I see another post here that states a room with a king bed was only $125 a night. I don't know why my price was higher. They also recommend that you tip the maid $3 per day. I usually tip the maid, anyway, but I just felt like they were nickle and diming me with this suggested tip as well. Make it $173 per night. I have never given a bad review to a hotel on trip advisor before, and I still highly recommend Wind Chimes Inn if you are looking for a hotel in the Condado area. I felt the service and the people there were wonderful, and I didn't feel like I was getting less value for my money.

<Author>ponsib
<Content>Nice location while visiting San Juan My family of four recently stayed at the Coral Princess Inn which is conveniently located in Condado. It is easy to catch a bus or cab to Old San Juan from this location. The beach is a short walk away and there are many restaurants to choose from. Our room with one queen size bed was very small, especially when we added the roll away mattress. If I knew how small the room was I would have reserved a different one. The room was clean however and we didn't have problems with the hot water supply when we wanted it. The property is maintained nicely with many tropical plants. The area where breakfast is served is very nice. They offer the standard continental food and drinks. They also have a piano for the guests and a quiet reading room. The pool is very small but my kids still enjoyed it very much. They also have a hot tub on the upper level but you need to walk through the penthouse suite to get to it. Overall our experience was good while staying here and I would select it again if we return to San Juan.

<Author>joelsmama
<Content>Coral Princess a let-down We stayed in the Penthouse suite for one quick night, and on first impression it was very cool! Definitely a smooth decor: very modern. The whole hotel has a random chic appearance with antique furniture blended with bold colorful paintings and modern lines. Only upon settling in did we begin to be disappointed. The toilet paper, a priority for my D.H., was the cheapest quality one could purchase, the shower was plumbed directly into the jacuzzi tub, which was a little awkward to step in or out of, there were cheap soaps and, a female's favorite, conditioning shampoo. I don't know a female that doesn't appreciate conditioner!! There weren't even kleenex in the room! The cheap t.p. had to suffice! There were doors that opened directly onto the roof-top deck that had no instructions and were impossible to open. The a.c. was an individual unit mounted on the wall controlled by a remote that, apparently, had been dropped so the LCD screen was unreadable. I spent the night either roasting or freezing not being able to find a happy medium. Another disappointment for me was that the hotel was a $12 (one way) cab fare away from Old San Juan. The last, but not least, missing commodity in our PENThouse sute was an alarm clock!!!! All that said, the bed was very comfy, the staff friendly and the hotel fairly clean. Probably wouldn't stay there again, or wouldn't pay *$200* dollars for maybe what a lesser room would've offered.

<Author>usually_happy64
<Content>Great find We changed reservations and selected this hotel after reading reviews in Tripadvisor and Frommer's. The hotel was lovely with beautiful plantings and nice furnishings. The staff was uniformly helpful. The rooms were large enough and the bathroom, while small, had a jetted (standard size) tub as well as a shower. We especially like going to the roof after a day of sightseeing and soaking in the hot tub. The Coral Princess is in a good location with just a short walk to many restuarants or the bus stop, which provides easy access to Old San Juan. There is a rocky beach within a few blocks, but ask about the truly lovely beach slightly farther away which is next to another large hotel. Because of that hotel being there lounge chairs, towels and umbrellas can be rented on the beach, lunch can be order from wait staff who come to the beach and deliver and the very nice changing facilities and showers are open to the public.The breakfast was adequate, but nothing more. We were dissapointed that there was never any Caribbean fruit (only bananas). The pastries, yogurt and such were all from Costco. It was fine, but nothing special.We spent four night here and would not hesitate to return when we come back to Puerto Rico. A very good value for the money.

<Author>Bumpa2328
<Content>Very good stay We stayed here prior to a cruise. The room and staff were very good and the breakfast was very adequate. <Author>LauraGuth
<Content>Great little inn close to the action. My husband and I recently spent 2 nights at this inn. It is just one block off the main street in Condada, meaning it's close to the shopping, restuarants, casinos and beach. Our room was on the small side, but very comfortable. <Author>AndeanTraveler
<Content>Nice hotel, close to the beach I stayed in this hotel with my wife and small daughter for 8 days at the end of December. This is a clean and well-kept hotel with modern furniture in the rooms, flat-screen TV's with over 100 free cable channels, and a wine fridge in every room. A basic continental breakfast is included in the price. There is a jacuzzi in a nice terrace patio in the third floor that is open until 9 pm in the evening. There is also a small pool in the first floor of the hotel, but it's not very sunny there. As far as we can tell, this is not a chain hotel, which is good because the staff were that much more friendly. We asked for a crib for our daughter and were provided with one free of charge. There is a very good Argentinian restaurant called Buenos Ayres just down the street with very tasty food and large portions at a moderate price ($18 to $25 per main dish). The beach is two blocks away. NOTE OF CAUTION: if you go to San Juan (or most other places on the north shore) during the winter months from December to March, the ocean rough - the waves are strong and the undertow is powerful. While we were in Condado beach we saw an emergency situation in which a person got too far out from the shore and had to be rescued by several other people. Afterwards we were told by some locals that this (and worse) happens several times each winter. Be careful.

<Author>cruzr4ever
<Content>It was great... We booked the Coral Princess for one night pre-cruise. Upon arriving to the Inn, they told us we were upgraded to the pent house suite. Wow- we're never that lucky. Large, spacious room , lots of marble, jacuzzi/shower combo. View isn't great, Condado is up and coming, some of the buildings are rough. We found a neat little resturant nearby called Latin Star. Yum. The staff at the Coral Princess are very knowledgable and friendly. They held our luggage the following morning after checkout so we could check out the area, and go to the beach. The beach by the way was rough, and not conducive to swimming. There are some impressive stores also very near, Ferragamo, Vuitton, Dior, etc if your budget allows. The complimentary breakfast was just as described by others. Plenty of choice, and a nice atmosphere in which to enjoy. Would stay with them again. About 15 minutes to the cruise pier via taxi.

<Author>EWHawk
<Content>Loved the Coral Princess Date: Oct. 8, 2007Reviewer: E Hawk, South Carolina, USAMy wife and I stayed overnight at the Coral Princess while waiting on a cruise. We wish we could have stayed longer. The hotel is an excellent value, and the staff could not have been more pleasant. The only negative is that the rooms are a bit small. But, they are VERY comfortable, and totally clean. The A/C worked perfectly, which is an important item judging by reviews of other places. Internet service is available in the room, and the TV, while small, has plenty of channels and great reception. The area offers so much to do, you may not watch much. We didn't.The area is loaded with restaurants. We'd never been to Puerto Rico, and wanted to try local dishes. The staff recommended the Cafe d'Angel (I hope I spelled it right.), which was very close by. It was superb! Try the mifungo. You won't regret it. The hotel also serves a Continental Breakfast which was very good. The Condado Beach is only an easy 2 minute walk. Shopping is nearby, as you are close to a main thoroughfare. We felt comfortable walking in the area, even at night. Everyone we met was friendly and helpful, and no one seemed to mind speaking English. Some reviewers had different opinions on that, and perhaps we were simply more fortunate. I think tho', if you are pleasant to the people there, they will respond the same.As I said, we only stayed overnight, so we can't give a complete description of everything. I do know that if we return to San Juan (which we hope to do), we definitely plan on staying at the Coral Princess again.

<Author>Cynthia_Guy
<Content>What a wonderful surprise! A must-stay in San Juan! WOW! The Coral Princess Inn was more than we imagined! My husband I stayed at the Coral Princess our first week of our honeymoon and we could not have been more pleased. When we checked in, Janisse greeted us with a smile and informed us that we had been upgraded to the King Suite since it was our honeymoon! (I communicated with the hotel via email before our visit and found everyone to be extremely helpful). Janisse and Glenda were particularly helpful and pleasant during our entire stay!! We expected the rooms to be extremely small, however, found our room to be more than ample. We were in room #24 which is on the second floor in the back area of the hotel. We definitely recommend requesting one of these rooms. The floors are marble throughout the room and bathroom. The bathroom had a shower/tub combo and the tub had jacuzzi jets which was a pleasant surprise as well. The closet/wardrobe has drawers and provides limited space for hanging clothes. The courtyard area was beautiful and the continental breakfast each morning was more than sufficient (croissants, ham, cheese, waffles, oatmeal, juices). The room had a mini fridge stocked with beer, water and wine. The bottles of water were only $1 and the beer was $2 which is much less you would expect for a minibar. One note - they do not have a full size ironing board in your room, so be prepared to use a small tabletop board if you must iron. The location of the hotel is perfect - we ate at 2 great restaurants on Magdalena (hotel's street): Cieto Lindo (Mexican) and Ramiros (fine dining). The beach is about a 3 minute walk straight up from the hotel. Walgreens, as everyone mentioned is right around the corner and open 24 hours. The bus (B21) drops you off almost right in front of the hotel. Note: if you ride the buses make certain to have change as they don't accept bills or credit cards.So, all said and done, we definitely recommend this hotel and if we return to San Juan will stay again at the Coral Princess Inn. Enjoy!Guy  Cynthia Willis, Oklahoma

<Author>ankh1234
<Content>Beautiful hotel and excellent location at a good price. This hotel is the main reason my wife and I enjoyed our trip to Puerto Rico. It was our first time there, August 4th thru 10th, and probably our last. We chose this hotel because of all the great reviews and its in between all the places we wanted to visit. We visited the caves on the west side and biobay on the east side and the rain forest - which is a must. And Old San Juan too which is just a bunch of shopping except for the two forts.First off, we picked up our rental car and drove towards the hotel. People in Puerto Rico tend to drive fast and change lanes often. Growing up in a big city, I'm used to congestion but changing lanes without signals and very often is a little unnerving. Anyway, we found that we missed our turnoff for the hotel and ended up in Old San Juan. No big deal, the street turns around there due to ocean and takes you right back to Condado and basically straight to the hotel on the one way street. They only have 4 spaces in front of hotel or parking at a lot one block down. We arrived around 1 pm and all the spaces were empty. (We only had to park in the $10 lot one day). Check in was fast and courteous. No problems. Had a room on 2nd floor and perfect size for two people. Nice little refrig. for stowing leftovers and pop purchased at Walgreens right around the corner. Simple breakdown.Hotel was very good price and great location.Only 4 free parking spaces and usually filled up by 5 pm.$10 daily parking one block away if you show ticket to front desk.Walgreens one block away to meet all essentials.Beach two blocks away and very nice with good waves.Good choice of restaurants within walking distance.Recommend Via Appia for italian and Piu Bella for a great selection of sandwiches.Plenty of police around and never felt worried about safety.If you look for change on the ground, you will be happy, we found two dollar bills, about 30 pennies, a nickel, about 5 dimes and a sterling silver ring. Its always good to be aware of your surroundings. Adds to the adventure of life and helps the pocket book. Buses are hit and miss. I'd recommend a taxi for old San Juan or short drive with rental car but make sure you park in free spot. Not well marked and saw alot of tickets. $75 dollar ticket.(Gas was .70 a liter)breakfast included and had meat, bread, pastry, oatmeal, cereal, juice, yogurt and some other things. Perfect filler before heading out on day trips.Pool is small but clean. Hot tub has alot of jets. Plenty of nooks to read books in or chat. Chaise lounges on 3rd floor for sunning.Room was cleaned around 2:30 pm.Front desk always glad to help.If I ever wanted to go back to Puerto Rico, I'd definitely stay here again!!!

<Author>travelKC
<Content>cozy, affordable and close to the best of PR We stayed at this little hotel for three days of our honeymoon after reading reviews on TripAdvisor and I must say, we were not disappointed. Some of the reviews had been mixed, and we had trouble deciding upon an affordable hotel in the San Juan area. We knew we wanted to stay in a boutique hotel, not a huge resort full of families and this fit the bill.The hotel is conveniently located to lots of shops and restaurants and it's just a short trip to Old San Juan where we spent several of our days. The rooms are aiming for a contemporary style and the bathrooms were nicely sized. The one disappointment was that our room was not at all near ready upon our arrival, despite my confirming our arrival time prior to our trip. The attendant at the front desk tried to be accomodating and put our bags in the hotel office while we wandered around. We came back a little while later and our room still was not ready, and the maid was standing around, not cleaning. Finally, the room was ready and the clerk did give us a discounted rate for our trouble.Despite the rocky start, our visit was great. THe small pool in the side yard is charming, but don't expect to be able to swim laps. The rooftop deck was great, though i've heard it's not accessible if someone has rented the penthouse (which is on the same floor). We attempted to soak in the hottub one evening, but the chemicals weren't balanced and it wasn't particularly enticing for that reason.Breakfast was perfect--coffee and croissants. Just a little continental treat.This place was a great bang for the buck, especially if you're like us and spend all of your time out sight-seeing.

<Author>LeftenantMonterey_CA
<Content>Just Right If your looking for a small intimate hotel nestled in a city neighborhood, versus the high rises on the beach with casinos etc, this is an excellent choice. We spent the last night of our Vieques-Culebra vacation at the Coral Princess in the Condado neighborhood of San Juan. It's two blocks from the beach and shops, and five or ten minutes from the airport. Room with Queen bed was $115 but taxes made it about $142. The hotel was renovated about 6 years ago with Mexican tiles in the courtyard and marble in the bath, colorful art throughout. Nice grotto with palms, pool, and breafast area (included in the room price). Staff was friendly and helpful recommedning an excellent restaurant a couple blocks away Marisqueria Miro where we dined on fabulous Catalonian seafood with wonderful Spanish red wine (Arzuage Crianza 2004) recommended by our lively waiter Marcello. Good bed. Good Value. We really liked it.

On the 2 occasions we requested a taxi/cab one came promptly.On our last visit to San Juan we stayed at the Comfort Inn a few streets away. This was just as conveniently located and was definitely better value for money. If we return to San Juan in the future we will stay at the Comfort Inn.

<Author>SnCollins
<Content>Not as great as everyone says... My husband and I stayed here for four days after a vacation in Vieques. The hotel is okay from the outside and located in a nice, mostly residential neighborhood. It truly is one block from a very pretty beach, and is close to a lot of the restaurants and bars, along with casinos/ATM's/Internet cafes, etc in Condado. It is a $12.00 cab ride to Old San Juan, or there is rumored to be a trolley and buses, but we saw no trolleys (ever) and only a few buses. We found the taxis, though more expensive, to be much more convenient. Their rates are set in the tourist zones of Condado, OSJ, Isla Verde, etc. The rate to the airport is $17.00. Regarding the hotel, we were surprised to see how small everything was. The pictures made it look bigger and from the reviews I read, I didn't recall reading this. Rooms: Our room was the smallest room I had ever stayed in by far. We saw other rooms on the first floor while the maids were cleaning and all were very small. We stayed in Room 6. We paid $153 a night with taxes and other fees. I judged that it was about 11'x12', plus a VERY small bathroom. The jacuzzi tub is a bathtub, only large enough for one person, with a couple of jets. We had one queen bed, a desk, and a minibar in the room. No storage for suitcases, very little room to hang or store clothes. There was one piece of nice art and that is the best thing I can say about the room. The bed was average and the linens were scratchy. By far the worst thing about the room was that it was terribly loud. It is located, along with several other rooms, right off the pool, the breakfast area, and the area where the maids park their cleaning supply cart for the entire morning. If you plan on sleeping past 6:30 in the morning at this hotel, don't stay there, or ask for a quieter room on the second or third floor. The first two mornings we were awakened by plates in the breakfast area, and then by our upstairs 'neighbors' sliding around chairs and walking around in high heels. Very frustrating. Keep in mind this is a small hotel and you are literally paying for a bedroom, not an actual hotel room. The living areas are nice, and they apparently expect you to your time in them or outside the hotel. Service: Housekeeping does a very nice job. Everyone at the hotel was very friendly and helpful. Check-in was easy.Living Areas: There is a lovely patio off of the reception area and some of the rooms. The pool and breakfast area are off the back side of the patio. The pool is extremely small, has four chairs, and is surrounded by barbed walls. It's not overly usable, but will keep you cool. On the third floor there is a nice kitchen w/ frig, microwave, etc that can be used by guest, a pool table, dining table, and an outside patio with a table/chairs and hot tub. Dining/Drinks: There is a minifridge in the room with beer/wine/soda. The prices are very reasonable, although we never used it. The breakfast is from 7:00-10:00 I believe, and is yogurt, fruit, ceral, lunchmeat, croissants, coffee, and orange juice. There are several restaurants around the hotel that are average. Overall our impression of the restaurants in San Juan was not good. We had the worst meal I've ever had anywhere at Mofongos, down along the water at the cruise piers in Old San Juan. We paid $70 for two of the worst meals I've ever seen and my husband was very sick that night after dinner. Excursions: We rented a car from Avis, just down the street, for $55 a day including insurance and drove ourselves out to see the Camuy Caves (note they are not open on Monday or Tuesday). The caves are absolutely amazing and shouldn't be missed! It is $12.00 pp to get in and $3.00 to park. Plan on waiting unless all trolleys are up and running (unlikely). The Marriott offers this same tour for $120 a person, or there are independent companies that charge $60-$70pp. We also saw the Oricebo Observatory and Museum. Definitely worth it also, but might be very difficult for those who are out of shape or handicapped....it's 500+ steps to get up to the museum and overlook. I believe it was $5.00 per person to get into the museum.Overall, the hotel is really just average. If you plan on being up very early and don't mind SMALL spaces, the hotel might be okay for you. If I were to go back, I would choose the Hotel Milano in Old San Juan (it's cheaper and in a better location, not to mention nicer) or one of the hotels on the beach in Condado and pay the difference. I would not stay here again.

<Author>siamesecat2965
<Content>Great little hotel! Stayed here the night before and night after our cruise (May 5 and 13). Nice, clean, no frills hotel. Rooms are comfortable, although not overly large, but with nice flat panel tvs, jacuzzi tubs, lots of nice fluffy towels, etc.Each room also has a wine chiller, stocked with water, soda ($1 each) and space to keep your own drinks cool.Staff was VERY accomodating. Held our luggage after check-out while we played tourist in Old San Juan, and also on our return after the cruise. Arrived before 9am after cruise, and they not only held the luggage, but offered breakfast, bottled water, and allowed us to sit by the pool.Staff is very friendly and helpful, will call you a cab, recommend places to eat, etc. Area has lots of restaurants, plus 24 hour Walgreens around the corner. About 2 blocks away is an internet cafe, which i used to check in for my flight and print boarding pass. The beach is about 3 blocks, and the bus to OSJ (.75 each way) picks you up around the corner, and the return stop is across the street.prices were lower than some of the big resorts closer to the pier, and i believe it was about $16 to the pier by taxi, well worth it, in my opinion.Didn't use the pool or hot tub, but they are clean and well kept...

<Author>ae82
<Content>Pleasantly surprised After doing weeks and weeks of seaching for a hotel in San Juan, my girlfriend and I picked the Coral Princess Inn.Hotel: We stayed on the first floor. The hotel is very clean, and has a great atmosphere. We had a Queen sized bed in our room, and found that there was ample space for our 2 suitcases. You get a small wardrobe which was very handy. There's also a small fridge. The bathroom isn't large, but nor is it cramped. Breakfast was great, and we had many items to pick from. It was cheaper for us to book directly through the hotel.Staff: Very friendly and helpful. Customer service was excellent. Can't ask for much more.Location: About 2 blocks from the beach, and there are many great restaurants nearby. They aren't cheap, but perfect for a nice dinner. There is also a nearby Walgreens which was very convenient. We only took walks on the beach at night, so I have no idea how nice Condado beach is. The hotel property is also easily accessible from the highway. Watch out for rush-hour San Juan traffic. Here's a hint: Go to east (Fajardo, etc) during the weekday. Save going west for weekends. We found that to work very well for us.Parking: We had a rental car all 4 days of our trip. There are 3 spots infront of the hotel, and only 1 night we were lucky enough to get it. Otherwise, we parked at a nearby parking lot down the street for $10 a day. It's steep, but expected.Overall: It's great that this hotel isn't a large hotel with bustling with tourists. We loved how at home you feel once you've setteled in. Very unique, and I would definitely be a return visitor.

<Author>lakesideliving
<Content>Affordable luxury My travel agent recommended this place. We needed a place to stay one night after finishing a 7 night cruise. Definitely a gem. Somehow we were given the Penthouse 1. <Author>bluegrassky
<Content>Terrific inn, newly renovated and charming! We stayed at this hotel for one night as we returned to San Juan from a cruise and it was excellent. Our room and bathroom were large and the common areas beautifully decorated. Floors throughout are tile and there are many art pieces on the walls and in specially designed niches. On the main floor is a garden and patio area which is simply breathtaking, with orchids and other tropical plants. Once away from the front desk, you would hardly know you were still in the middle of a large city. There is also a small pool which has been built into a secluded area; a small elevator; and in the back of the main floor, a piano, a breakfast bar, and a microwave. Our room had a refrigerator and internet access.Personally, I would probably not choose this inn if I was traveling with children, mainly because the atmosphere seems better suited to couples or solo travelers. Some areas would also be difficult to navigate with a stroller or extra luggage. The Old Town is a short drive or taxi ride away, and there are a number of good restaurants within walking distance. There is a US post office and a drugstore with grocery items about a block away. The staff was exceptionally accommodating and followed up with us immediately on an item we had left behind. We would definitely recommend this inn to anyone looking for an oasis in the middle of San Juan...it was the perfect end to our vacation.S. Rey-Barreau

<Author>Drifting_clouds
<Content>A very pleasant stay We stayed at this hotel after spending a few nights at the dismal pit known as the Iberia Hotel. What a wonderful relief it was to move here! For only about $50 more the experience was a huge step up. The Coral was modern and well appointed. Lots of attractive plants and everything seemed airy and open. The room had a nice king bed, a fridge, a flat screen TV and a jetted tub. The breakfast was served buffet style outside and was an unexpected treat as we didn't know that was included. We had stayed at the Caribe Hilton in SJ a few weeks before and for more than double the price had no breakfast, so this breakfast was a nice addition and had a big selection. The pool is small but nice to jump into when you get hot walking the streets shopping. The staff was attentive to questions but not chatty. All in all I would definitely recommend this hotel.

<Author>milril44
<Content>Almost perfect For our first trip to San Juan, going by the mostly positive reviews here, I found the Coral Princess Inn to be almost perfect. We stayed in room 15 which was fairly large, clean and adequate. Marble floors and bathroom, mini fridge, a/c and ceiling fan, flat panel tv's. The upstairs open lounge area was very nice, although we didn't get a chance to use it. The pool, which we did use, was small, but very nice. They stored our luggage until our room was ready. The included breakfast was nice.The day time desk person was knowledgeable about the area, but the evening person was not so much. The beach was only two blocks away. Taxi to the airport seemed to cost about $15 + bag fees. Taxi to Old San Juan is $12. I can highly recommend Via Appia on Ashford Ave, it is a Italian and pizza neighborhood joint filled with locals and the food and service are excellent. Walgreens was close by and very handy.I only have two complaints. The hotel is in the Condado area. There is not a whole lot in the Condado area aside from a three-four block stretch of restaurants and stores on Ashford Ave. If you wandered even a block or two outside of the touristy area, it got really seedy and there were a lot of homeless beggars around. The other complaint is that the water pressure in the shower was non-existent, a very weak spray and the water kept changing temperature throughout the shower, so you were either freezing or scalded repeatedly. Aside from these two problems, the Coral Princess Inn would have been perfect.

<Author>Assateague_Bum
<Content>A Great Boutique Hotel Before booking our hotel in San Juan, I read many reviews of the Coral Princess Inn in TripAdvisor.com. Of the several dozen I read, around 95% were very positive and the rest were mostly good. I am glad to report that our experience was also very positive.First the pros: The Coral Princess Inn is very pretty and well maintained. The hotel is small (boutique), but is decorated with many tropical plants (especially on the outside areas) and has several nooks for reading or other semi-private conversations. The appointments are very nice dark wood, reminicent of an English style The pool area is quite attractive as well. My wife loved the morning coffee and continental breakfast area where people would gather each morning. Plus, the dishes were china, not plastic - a very nice touch!Our room was small, but again, nicely appointed and very, very clean. And the tub was a jacuzzi tub, which was unexpected.The hotel is in the Condado area, in sort of a neighborhood area, a bit off the beaten path but only a few blocks from the beach and touristy stuff. We very much appreciated that part. Several restaurants were within a block or so of the hotel as was a Walgreen's (which also had a grocery section!) which was certainly helpful. The staff were all very helpful and friendly. We stayed at the hotel for 4 nights and our airconditioner stopped cooling on the 3rd night (not a big deal considering how mild the temps were). I reported the problem that morning as we were leaving for an excursion and the staff had it repaired in a matter of a few hours - very impressive!The only thing I can think of for improvement is that printed bus schedules/routes be made available for the guests. For some reason, you can't find these anywhere at hotels, Not sure what the story is with that.To be honest, we were not that impressed with San Juan as a destination. The beaches were blah (no one even bothered to have the seaweed cleaned off the beaches), the concept of beach bars seemed to be almost completely lost on the local tourist industry and the food and drink quality was fairly low, yet prices were rather high. I doubt we will go back to San Juan, but we might try other areas of Puerto Rico.Of course, the above negatives have virutally nothing to do with the Coral Princess Inn. They were absolutely the highllight of our trip and my wife and I would highly recommend them to anyone traveling to San Juan.  
<Date>Mar 23, 2007

<Author>G+10
<Content>Good deal We stayed at the hotel for two nights after a cruise. We arrived at the hotel about 11:00 am, and our room was not ready. They allowed us to put our luggage in a room so we could go walk about until our room was ready. We went to eat at a place right around the corner. Stopped in at Walgreens for some tanning lotion, and then we headed back to the hotel about 1:00 pm. They got us into our room. The room was clean, spacious, and comfortable. They have a frig in the room that has soda, water, beer, and wine for very affordable prices. $2 for beer and $1 for water. You could also place items in there that you brought yourself. We got changed and hit the beach 2 blocks away. Clean and spacious beach. Rented two chairs. We took a bio-luminescense bay tour that night. The breakfasts in the morning were sufficient and just like many others have commented on. The second day we went on an El Yunque tour and then tanned on the top floor of the hotel where the hot tub is located. Very relaxing. The pool is very small and hard to get any sun. We went to the Marriott for drinks that evening and dinner at the Japanese restaurant next door to the Marriott. Certainly not an upscale hotel (we actually got picked up for one of our tours at the Ritz-Carlton...NICE), but it was clean, pretty and affordable. If you aren't looking for a resort, this hotel is right for anyone.

<Author>Prodigal_Hoosier
<Content>Cute and cozy, but small. Do not expect luxury. We spent four nights at the Coral Princess. The staff were friendly and helpful. The room was very small. The bed not particularly comfortable. The sheets were anything but crisp. The pillows were small and flat. The best part of the Inn is outside the room. The environs are warm and cozy, and secluded. There seemed to be few people about, but the Inn was full. Breakfast was totally lame. We will only return to the Coral Princess if we are going with a group of friends or family. The third floor has a nice, roomy area with a large dinner table, sofas, and a full kitchen that would be great for evening get togethers with friends to swap stories from the day of site seeing and beach going. The nearby beach was clean and provided us plenty of room even during this spring break week.I highly recommend the area and the beach, but will choose a more full featured hotel on our next trip.

<Author>anneloo
<Content>what a little princess! We stayed for one night at the coral princess inn and wished we had stayed longer. The property itself is a a hidden jewel in the jaded district of condado.We had a double room on the front of the property |(yes it gets a little noisy but who stays in their rooms that long anyway??) which had a flat screen tv, two large windows and a full bathroom with jacuzzi tub...a real treat after a nights dancing. Lovely rooms full of characterWe tried the pool on arriving but the sun had gone in over this part of the hotel...I would suggest going straight to the 3rd floor and sit in the hot tub watching the world go by in condado. Breakfast, although some may say it was a little basic was more than adequate for us, fresh orange, serve yourself toast cereal, coffee and pastries...just what you needed to set you up forthe day. It was all fresh and there was plenty to eat if you were really hungryI have to say I thougt this hotel was, in comparison to some of the larger, brasher hotels in condado, a lovely place which does the owners proud. From the rooms to the beautful terraces and gardens throughout it cannot fail to please (and if it does stick to the souless larger hotels on Ashford Avenue)I would have no hesitation in staying there again, its a lovely hotel with a location that is in the middle of everything you need to see in Condado.

<Author>travelgal50
<Content>nice property-great location My 13 year old daughter and I recently spent 2 nights at the Inn pre-cruise. We found the previous reviews to be accurate. The Inn is similar to staying in a villa witha private pool, multiple sitting areas, a reading room, rooftop terrace etc. The location is excellent- close to restaurants ( angel cafe for puerto rican food, Danne's for Italian), the beach ( about a block and one half), salons (pedicure/manicure), and multiple shopping venues. There is a great little gelato place right around the corner that is good for a light lunch. My daughter basically had the pool all to herself which was great after a day of sightseeing . The breakfast was more than adequate with croissants, cold cereal, yogurt, ham, cheese, pastries, juices, and wonderful coffee. The room itself was a bit small ( we had 2 double beds, a whirlpool tub, flat screen TV, microwave, and small fridge, but was certainly adequate to our needs. The mattresses on the beds were a bit uncomfortable and should probably be replaced. Other than that we found our stay at the Inn to be pleasant and would recommend it without hesitation.

<Content>Cute - but........... After reading reviews through trip advisor we booked a three night pre-cruise stay at the Coral Princess Inn. The hotel is very cute and very, very clean with lots of nice areas around the hotel for sitting and relaxing. The breakfast area was very nice. I will say though that we had the smallest hotel room (#8) we have ever stayed in. There was a double bed with barely enough room to walk around it - in fact, we both banged our shins on the corners of the bed several times. There was no closet, only a small armoire with 2 hangers. We did not unpack our suitcases - there was no room. We thought we better get used to it as we were going to an inside cabin on the ship - but believe me, that was way bigger! On the last day, we were able to store our bags in a locked room for the afternoon with a bunch of other luggage (very convenient).All in all, it is a cute hotel...........fine to stay in for a night or two, but I sure wouldn't plan a weeks holiday there - at least not in that room. The $120 US night charge, with taxes, ended up costing $181.71 per night Cdn. - reasonable I guess for Puerto Rico, but................

<Author>MJ24
<Content>Great Little Inn in the heart of Condado Recently stayed there with my mom (2/8-2/13) and knew we would have a great time based on all of the reviews I had read. I was pleasantly surprised at how quaint this inn is. Our room was on the second floor towards the back (#21) and it was so nice and quiet and peaceful. Felt like home. In the morning my mom would drink her coffee outside in the little outdoor sitting area. At night after dinner we would sit upstairs on the third floor to wind down.Breakfast in the morning was nice. Never found it crowded as others have mentioned. And if they did find it crowded, there's always space upstairs on the 2nd floor where you can sit and eat and read the paper if you like.Pool area was small but then again, if you wanted a hotel with a big pool then you should stay somewhere else like the Marriott. You get what you pay for. This inn is nicely priced without all of the big hotel craziness and that's what we liked about it.The beach is only 2 blocks away (watch out though, the surf is a bit rough) and you can rent chairs for $3. While there the beach was not crowded and the weather was fantastic, sunny and in the 80s. There was always a police presence either at the beach or around town so we always felt safe.Walgreens is a block away and as others have mentioned so is the bus stop to head into San Juan. The schedule is a little sketchy (we waited 20 min to go to San Juan and 30 min to head back to Condado in the afternoon). There are tons of restaurants on Ashford Av and nice little shops. Mom already wants to go back she loved it so much. Definitely recommend this inn if you are looking for something quiet and close to everything.

Having read all the reviews, there were a few things that we didn鈥檛 expect. The rooms are small and have no closets, only a half sized armoire. There are no security safes in the room, you have to rent them. There were none available our whole stay. The pool only has space for about three sun recliners. When the hotel is at capacity the breakfast area can get very crowded and seating is a problem. All in all it is a nice little property within walking distance to three beaches: Condado (great for kids), Ocean Park (long stretch of sand with warm water but rough surf) and the beach around the corner that has chairs for rent. It is also central to all the night life. The area seemed very safe to us.

<Author>lcosette
<Content>just right! Coral Princess Inn was the perfect little hotel for us. It was in a great location, about 3 blocks from the beach, 2 blocks from walgreens, 2 blocks from the bus to old san juan, and surrounded by lots of restaurants and shops. There are also other larger hotels, such as the mariott, nearby if you want to take advantages of things such as spa services or casinos. We stayed at the Coral Princess Inn for 5 nights, and the price was incredibly reasonable for what we received. The room was small, but was clean and the bathroom and floor were marble, which was nice. We had cable and high-speed internet access. There are many places to sit, and a nice walkway with lots of plants. The hotel has a small pool and hot tub which we didn't use, and breakfast every morning from 7-9 which i never woke up early enough to use, but my friend said the breakfast was 'okay'. This is not a luxury hotel, so don't expect lots of amenities. But you can expect all of the basics a hotel should have.overall, i'd definitely stay here again because of the location, cleanliness, friendly staff and mostly because of the price.

<Author>Hombregrandedearuba
<Content>Beautiful Little Inn We stayed at the Coral Princess Inn last weekend, after reading several reviews on this site. The location is great, extremely central in the Condado area, just 1,5 block away from the Marriott Hotel, and two blocks from the beach. Walgreens is right around the corner, for any little groceries. Being a manager in a 4-Star Renaissance hotel in the Caribbean, I can say that I know where I'm talking about: The hotel has a small reception, with staff that is helpful, and are willing to do an extra step for you. The 25 rooms are among 3 floors, of which the topfloor is the nicest, with the biggest rooms(suites), some sort of living room(nicely maintained), a pooltable, and a outside area with loungchairs and a jacuzzi. On the ground floor, where our room was located, the place is full of plants, (maybe even too full), which gives a very comfortable cozy atmosphere. Breakfast happens there, on nicely maintained furniture.The room we were in was Nr.10, which is actually a room for disabled, so we had no jacuzzi but a shower, which worked out OK. The hotel was full, so there was no choice as to stay in that room. The rooms have a fridge, microwave, a TV, a good airco-unit, but no cutlery in the drawers under the microwave... The fridge was filled with some beverages , which were very cheap ($1,- for Soda, $2,- for beer). The turndown service was up to 4/5 star standard, with daily refreshment of towels, etc... Moreover, which is in my opinion the most important, the place was clean and well maintained, both inside as outside the rooms!The breakfast, which is included, consists daily(!) of: OJ, Coffee, Milk, Flakes, Croissants, 3 kinds of pastries, ham/cheese, yoghurts, marmelade, bananas. Good enough to start your day with. But for a week stay it would be a little boring.The one little difficulty is parking, with only four spots in front of the hotel. My Puerto Rican friend had to park her car everytime on parking lot Magdalena, which is one block away, and is $10,65 for 24 hours. That's the best deal you can get closeby, or you might wanna choose to go and find yourself a spot in the nearby streets.If you are used to big hotels and robotic service, go to those places, and pay double of what you pay here; a nice, cozy and clean(!) place, on a great location and TOP value for money. Have fun!!

<Content>Loved this hotel! We just got back from a long weekend at this hotel and we loved it. We loved the hot tub on the roof and spent almost every night up there for sunset. The staff was superb. They helped us with directions, restaurant recommendations, and set up a tour of El Yunque for us. My boyfriend especially appreciated Jose's help. The room was really nice and clean and was a bit small but we spent very little time in it. Yes, the water temperature does fluctuate a bit, but honestly, it's not a big deal. Our room had a fridge where you could purchase cheap bottles of water and soda. My boyfriend thought there was a bit too much hallway noise, but compared to other hotels I've stayed at I think it was pretty minimal. There was a continental breakfast which was completely purchased things from Costco, but it was adequate. And they served it until 10:00 which was nice. Finally, the pool is small, but was very cute and nice. It is shaded in the afternoon, which was nice for me with my fair skin. There were plenty of nice outdoor spaces to relax, a reading room, a pool table, a kitchen, and laundry facilities.

<Author>admglick
<Content>nice place, helpful staff, great location I would agree with the generally positive reviews of the Coral Princess. It is a nice, small property in a great location. They are a few blocks from many restaurants, 2 blocks from the beach and 1 block from Wallgreens (in case you forgot anything!)The rooms were ok. nothing special, but about what you would expect for this price and they were clean. The best parts of the place were the location and the very friendly and helpful staff who work there.Breakfast is very simple, but fine and in a nice setting. there is a great deal of common and outdoor space for a hotel of this size. in fact, the number of nice sitting areas almost seems excessive if that is possible. There is a hot tub on the roof which is very nice, but when we went to use it, it was cold! The staff said they couldn't do much to fix it, so we didn't try it again.One other strange complaint is that the lobby was always cold. The lobby is very small and is just basically the check in desk and the elevator, so you don't spend much time there, but I felt bad for the staff who had to work there, they all seemed to bring sweaters and sweatshirts. I would definitely stay here again when visiting PR. The place had some minor issues, but it was clean, charming, helpful staff and in a great location at a great price compared to other options around.

<Author>seg110
<Content>Perfect combo - Hip hotel without the attitude This is a BEAUTIFUL hotel without any of the too cool attitude you might expect from a property with original artwork all over. The staff is friendly but not overbearing, the rooms are very clean, bright, and provide enough space for two people and their luggage spread all over. The courtyard garden is truly exquisite - really a pleasure to walk through and sit in. Coral Princess Inn is a great hotel that is very affordable. There are a few parking spots in front, which is nice because the street parking is limited.Breakfast is everything you need it to be: coffee, juice, pastries, croissants, ham, cheese, bread, cereal, fruit. There is a toaster as well as microwave. The hotel also provide a unique 3rd floor suite that everyone can use. We enjoyed the jacuzzi as well as the pool table. The hotel also has a cute pool. All this in a EXTREMELY well-priced, boutique style hotel.It is literally 1 block to Condado beach which has really soft sand and big waves. Great for body surfing or boogey boarding, You are also around the corner from Ashford Avenue, which is the main drag in Condado. I would recommend taking a taxi (about $13) to Old San Juan for the day and walking around. It is really enjoyable to see the old architecture and forts, and there are fantastic shops there. I really recommend this hotel because it is between Old San Juan and the airport, yet has excellent beaches and won't break the bank while still providing continental breakfast. I will be staying here again, definitely, and so should you!

<Content>Wow, what a deal!!! We stayed for 2 nights. We booked it after reading reviews here, and going to the website. We were really impressed. What a great deal. <Author>SagarMung
<Content>Helpful staff, good location We booked this hotel for a weekend stay in San Juan. It is located on Calle Magdalena, which runs parallel to the main avenue, Calle Ashford. It's therefore close to all of the restaurants, bars, clubs, etc., but still quiet.There are about four to six parking spots available in front of the hotel, depending on how well the cars are squeezed together. There is street parking on side streets if you are up for looking, but you'll do yourself a favor by having a compact car. Parking rules in the area are marked, though sparingly, and since many people park illegally, you can't pick spots based on where others have parked.The hotel entrance is controlled by an electronic latch, so you must buzz in to enter. The front desk is staffed 24 hours, giving additional security. The staff was incredibly helpful and spoke both English and Spanish fluently.Hotel rooms are arranged around a small courtyard. We stayed in a Corporate Executive Queen. There was also a night table, dresser, TV, armoire, small fridge, microwave, and kitchenette sink. The bathroom also had a bath tub with jets. There was an internet router with a wired connection available, though we did not use it. The air conditioner and fan were powerful enough to get it cold (actually chilly).The continental breakfast was great, with yogurt, cinnamon and apple loaves, hamm, cheese, croissants, tea, and of course coffee. There is also a small in-ground pool on the property, though it could get crowded fairly quickly. The in-room fridge is stocked with water and soda for $1 each and beer for $2 each, which is only slightly more expensive than the same items at the Walgreen's right around the corner, but much cheaper than buying from vendors on the beach.The hotel is located in the Condado/Santurce area of San Juan, close to many restaurants and amenities. The beach is also only five minutes by foot, though we walked east a bit to find a less rocky portion.As another reviewer mentioned, the taxes add quite a bit to the published rate, but this is a result of local laws, not the hotel or the booking agency. On the whole, we had a good time at the hotel, and it served as a relaxing place to come back to every night. Our only complaint was that checkout time was at 11 a.m. instead of the usual noon.

<Author>D&DWorldTravelers
<Content>Good Deal, Great Service, Nice Stay We just returned from a five night stay at the Coral Princess and we enjoyed our stay. This is the perfect stop for the budget traveler. One thing to keep in mind when traveling in Puerto Rico tourist taxes add up. We didn't find out until we arrived at the hotel. The Expedia price said $99.00/night but with taxes it averaged out $140/ night. This is no fault of the hotel. We booked a room with a double bed for the two of us. It's small but we didn't plan on staying in the hotel much. There is free internet via ethernet cable. Apparently there is wireless but it was not working during our stay. The room was clean and the bed was comfy. There is a ceiling fan and a remote to the air conditioning unit. (The only reason I mention this is because it took some time to figure it out.) The only complaint about the room is the showerhead. It wasn't very strong but it's a very minor detail. As mentioned before on this site there are not many amenities but that did not bother us. The free breakfast was nice. There were fresh bananas, cereal, pastries, yogurt, and croissants. The front desk is very helpful. F.Y.I- If you plan on taking a bus to Old San Juan you need to take B21 and it does not seem to have a schedule. We waited 45 mins one day. The good thing is that it only costs 75 cents one way to Old San Juan. Otherwise expect to pay $12.00+ for cab fare. The beach is a block and a half away. There is plenty to eat in the surround neighborhood particularly on Ashford Ave.

<Author>sdtravelguy
<Content>Great Hotel I looked at various hotels on tripadvisor and decided to stay at the Coral Princess Inn, and am glad I did. I could not beat the price, location and service of this hotel. The hotel is about 2 blocks from Condado Beach, a block from a casino and within blocks of a few bars/clubs that I would frequent (alternative lifestyle). The room was very small, but was right off of a great little second floor patio that I could smoke and relax at. I had asked for an iron and ironing board and it was delivered in less than a minute.You have to be very careful what hotel you book in Condado, it is a great area, but has some questionable hotels. Stay at this one for a clean and convenient hotel.

<Author>wcwlc
<Content>Excellent location, friendly staff and great price Location: The hotel is located at Condado, which seems to me is going through some kind of transformation, there are some pretty run down building and new constraction at the area. During the day time, there isn't much going on. But at night it is hopping with great resturant and night lifes. We ate at some fabulas resturants that is just blocks from the hotel which is great because you cannot always find parking, if you do, you want to stay there. The hotel has arrangement with a local parking garage that is one block off for 10 per day. It is close and we don't mind the walk. The hotel only has two free parking athte front and it is almost always taken. We did walk to check out the beach that is two blocks off. With all the beaches in PR I have to give this a C+, it is kind of dirty and the surf is high. Other people has comment on the Walgreen. It is really one of the big selling point of this hotel for me. I am assuming people who read this are budget conscious and what is more budget conscious then purchasing your daily need in a chain store. I have to say we went to that store almost everyday we stay here. We purchase items such as sun block, lotion, disposible camera and etc. The price is a bit higher but not much more. There is also an internet cafe nearby for those of us who has to always stay connected but didn't want to carry the laptop. It is on Av. Ashe.Room: The hotel is create with the feeling of a boutique hotel. The furniture and design are very sleek and stylish(dark wood furniture with black and white marble tiles). However the hotel is really tiny and so are the room. My biggest complain is that there is no place to charge my laptop. The hotel has free internet connect but all the outlet has been taken (two for the lights at both end tables, one for the phone, one for the clock). So we had to live without the clock since that is the only one we can give up. Because the floor is marble tiled, there is a pretty significant crack at the bottom where the door and the tile floor touches (or doesn't touch), and we get bugs coming into the room all the time. We solve the problem by putting a towel over it. We do like the mini freg very much, we put our bottle water in it the night before so we can bring cold water with us.Amenity: The hotel has reading room, a kitchen, a piano, a tiled backyard with sitting area, 2nd floor sitting area and the third floor is like a club house with hot tub. It is really neat and we enjoy the breakfast. It has milk, orange juice, three or four different type of pastry, ham and cheese, bread and coffee (unfortunately they ran out of tea after the first day and never replace it. PR is not a big tea drinking country, not hot tea anyway). The pool is on the first floor hiding on the side of the building. It is tiny but during the two times we used the pool we are always the only one in it. It gave you the feeling that it is your own private pool so that is very nice.Service: People at Coral Princess Inn has provided excellent service. They listen to all our questions and did their best to help us. They do a great job clean the room everyday. When I had connection trouble they connected me with a helpdesk person right away and actually solved the problem in very little time.Misc: When we pick up our car in the Alamo, we were given a tourist map. The map actually mislabeled the hotel so you should try to print out your own direction instead of relying on the tourist map.

Hotel is a 15 dollar cab ride from airport, and a 2 minute walk from the Marriott, where you can use their casino and beach. Walgreens around the corner convenient for those things you forgot. All in all an excellent choice for a great price.

<Author>DCSM
<Content>good budget hotel we weren't at this hotel long - we got there at almost midnight and left at 7am the next morning for a snorkeling trip. then we returned at 5pm to pick up our stuff we had stored and left for our cruise. the hotel was nice though. a good budget place- though we were surprised about the taxes. we got a rate of 95 dollars, but with tax it was almost 140! that was surprising, but oh well. what can you do?the rooms are super super small. we could barely fit our two suitecases in there and still move around. the floor is a concrete tile and cold, but seemed clean. the bed looked a little sketchy - very worn linens - but was comfortable. but perhaps that was because i was so tired! :) the bathroom was small, but clean with a decent sized shower.the continental breakfast was better than basic, i though. we had ham and cheese croissant - very nice to start the day. they also had yogurt, juice and coffee. i was happy.the common area is beautiful and the staff is very helpful (stored our luggage all day and called taxis for us). the only thing is, the hotel is hard to get to because of traffic. it is on a one way street that is very congested. we wasted a lot of time stuck in taxis. and it is still 15 dollars to either old san juan or the pan american pier for the cruise. but as long as you know that, no biggie.

<Content>Very quaint and cultural! We stayed at the Coral Princess Inn for 3 days before our cruise departed from San Juan- At first, I was a bit skeptical, but once I entered the lobby, I loved it! <Content>Loved It I am a native to the Island currently living in Miami, Florida. All I have to say is that the Coral Princess highly exceeded my expectations. The hotel closely parallels the hotels you can find in South Beach. The rooms, although small, have high ceilings and large windows. There is a deck with a hot tub on the third floor and several lounge areas. The decor is very art deco and modern. The hotel was very clean and the staff went out of their way to make us feel at home. To our surprise the hotel provide free continental breakfast from 7:30 to 9:30. The hotel is walking distance to excellent restaurants, drug store, casino and beaches. You cannot go wrong !

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Highly Recommend the Coral Princess My boyfriend  I stayed at the Coral Princess for 2 nights in May, and were 100% satisfied. Of couse, it is not the Hilton, but I felt the $125/night we paid was a steal. The room was small, but very clean with tasteful decor. The bathroom was good sized, included a jacuzzi tub, and appeared to have been recently remodelled. The common areas of this hotel were absolutely beautiful. The complimentary breakfast was basic, but good. There is a small pool (which you should not need since the beach is two blocks away!) and on the third floor, a hot tub. The third floor also has a large, home-like common area with kitchen, living, dining, and pool table. We did not use this, but it looked really nice. The beach is so close, and the Marriott casino is right around the bend. This hotel has prime location and is a great place to stay if you don't want to pay the money for a busy resort-hotel. Cab rides into Old San Juan were short, less than ten minutes, and relatively cheap (I think it was 12 for both of us). Plaza Las Americas is about a 5 minute cab ride.

<Author>LenoxLJ
<Content>Great Boutique Hotel My husband and I stayed at this hotel for five nights in April 2006. The room was very quaint with an oil painting and nice furniture, with marble floors (a little small). Our room was very clean and I cannot relate to the other comments about being dirty. In fact, I thought it was above average with respect to cleaniness.The public areas and plants are simply lovely and very romantic.Our room faced the courtyard and it was at times noisy and I was awoken early in the morning and during an afternoon nap from loud guests sitting in the courtyard. I tried to change rooms, but there were no other options the first couple of nights. I was later showed some other rooms, but decided they were not as nice and/or bright as my room (Room 9) From my room, I had a wonderful view of the greenery, sunlight and sky.Although it was a little noisy, I would still highly recommend this hotel because the positives of the hotel clearly outweigh this small negative, especially considering the reasonable rates. I generally stay at five star hotels and thought this was a great alternative for a budget trip. In fact the staff was just as friendly as Four Seasons on the Big Island. They were wonderful, informative and soooo sweet. The owner was also very very nice.I recommend Angela's for dining which is a one minute walk from the hotel with great food and very reasonable prices. With respect to beaches, I would recommned walking down to Ocean Park. It's a local nice beach - very clean and swimmable. (about a 20 minute walk)

<Author>PatCoty
<Content>Wonderful Stay! The Coral Princess Inn was a breath of fresh air for us. I happened upon it while searching for a pre-cruise hotel with consistent good reviews here on Trip Advisor. Coral Princess Inn was everything we expected and more. The rooms were large and extremely clean. We had an executive room which was a bit larger than the standard for $10.00 more. Some may call the furnishings a bit austere, but for us, they were comfortable and just enough. The staff at Coral Princess Inn were friendly and so helpful. Desk Clerk, Jason, recommended at great restaurant for lunch just a block from the hotel and on our way back from the beach (a mere 2 blocks away!). The included breakfast was a terrific way to start the day, and was plentiful and very fresh. The small courtyard area was filled with tropical plants and flowering orchids, which continued the Caribbean atmosphere. The third floor had a lovely seating area and hot tub, as well as a small lap pool on the second floor. Suites were located on the 3rd floor and looked beautiful. I would recommend this hotel to anyone looking for clean, affordable, friendly, non-chain lodging in San Juan. We're looking forward to our next visit to the Coral Princess Inn.

<Content>Great for a short trip Our family (2 adults, 2 children) stayed at the Coral Princess in February. Overall it was quite a good experience. Our room had two double beds and was fairly small. The wardrobe was about 2ft wide by 2ft high, so a little small for the four of us. The bathroom was small and basic, but the kids loved the jacuzzi bath. There wasn't a coffee maker in the room which was a pity. There wasn't a room safe or iron/ironing board either.The guy on reception tried the 'hard sell' on excursions and kept phoning the room to see if we had made a decision! The tiny swimming pool was in the shade all afternoon, but the small hot tub on the roof was in a sun trap and was great.Breakfast was OK, nothing special, but quite edible.The aircon in the room was very noisy, but it was too warm to sleep without it.Would only recommend this hotel for a couple of nights at most. I would go back, but my husband wouldn't!
