<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>A Great Find! I've stayed at this small Inn twice, the first time was January '05 for three nights, and the second time for three nights this month. For me, it was a find as I tend to avoid high end American hotels, like the Marriott, with it's casino, tours, and overpriced food and drink. Ugh! As other reviewers have said, some rooms are small (mine was not) and very clean, but avoid Room #3, as it has no windows. I have found the staff to be knowledgable, helpful and friendly. Points that have not been mentioned in other reviews: there is a common seating area on the second floor for reading and coffee and a third floor deck with a hot tub. This, and sharing tables in the small breakfast area means that you naturally meet other guests from all parts of the U.S. and P.R. I enjoy this type of communal experience. It is a two block walk to the beach, and one block to Ashford Street where you can catch a bus into Old San Juan for $.75( $.35 for seniors). I have poked my head into several other budget hotels in the area (the Canarios and El Consulado) and I think the Coral Princess is the best of the bunch. I would definitely try to stay there again when I return to Puerto Rico.

<Author>mrvlv
<Content>Nice Find My friends and I spent one night here before a cruise and found the Coral Princess to be a quaint spot. The location is good, and for just a night or two, it's a great bargain. The artwork is gorgeous, the staff is pleasant and accomodating, and I loved the furniture designs. Others traveling with us were not thrilled with the small rooms, but my immediate group received a complimentary upgrade to one of the penthouse suites, and we were just fine. The whole upstairs area is great for entertaining if you have visitors while staying there. Overall, Coral Princess reminds me of European hotels--small with friendly staff and not too many extras. Not a 4 star, but I would definitely stay again, and I would recommend it for short stays.

<Author>CarolineinChicago66
<Content>Coral Princess is a Good Value in Coranando - not spectacular My husband and I, along with another couple in their 40's, stayed at this hotel in early January. POSITIVES: in the heart of Condado and just a 2 minute walk to beach. It's near the Marriott (WAY overpriced drinks at their outdoor bar, don't bother), Walgreens and within walking distance of a nice variety of restaurants. They also had a nice little buffet breakfast of fluffy croissants, cheese, ham, cereal, yogurt and wonderful P.R. coffee. It's a good deal given the location and what you get, nice smaller hotel with tiny pool (never used) and hot tub (that was only 85 degrees) NEGATIVES: rooms are small, marble floors in room (it may be just me, but I much prefer carpet), no view from room and they charge $1.00 just to pick up the phone. Also, this may be minor as well, but it was really tough to get the shower at a decent temperature -- it was either too hot or too cold.I would recommend this for people who won't be spending alot of time in their rooms (we didn't) and value budget over luxury. I've stayed at nicer smaller hotels, but this is fine, nothing great.Puerto Rico is wonderful! I'd highly recommend a snorkeling trip with East WInd Excursions to aqua clear island snorkeling and tours by Rafael to El Yunque Rain Forest. Isla Verde Beach is wonderful, just a few miles down. Old San Juan merits a morning visit as well.

<Author>Sneezie
<Content>A bit rough around the edges We stayed here for the last night during our trip to catch an early morning flight the next day. (We stayed near the rainforest the rest of the trip).The location is very convenient to Rt 26 which takes you to San Juan to the west, and the airport to the east. Having read all the raves on Tripadvisor prior to our arrival, however, I was slightly disappointed by the hotel. Our room was small (about 12x12). With a queen size bed, a desk and a TV cabinet, it felt crammed. I looked at two other rooms - one about the same size as ours with a queen size bed, and another that's bigger with a king size bed, for $20 more. I was told that all the rooms with queen beds are small. Since we were only staying for one night, we decided to keep our room.There was an unclean feel to the room that I couldn't quite place. Perhaps it was the heavy grain marble floor, or the dullness of it. For a new hotel, the furnishing was unexpectedly worn: the headboard rattled with the slightest movement in bed, and the paint on the desk was worn to bare wood in a few places. Perhaps what got to me the most was the dubious little black balls of lint/dirt in the bedsheet. We paid $130 with tax for one night. For longer stays, I recommend paying extra for a bigger room. However, for the same price, you could do better with some of the BB's or vacation rentals in the Condado/Ocean Park/Isla Verde area.A last word about parking - there are four parking spaces in front of the hotel, one of which is handicap reserved parking. If those are taken, parking is available at a nearby hotel for $10 every 24 hrs, or you may be able to find a spot on the street.

<Author>gwalt
<Content>Don't miss this one! The Coral Princess is a fabulous, boutique hotel in the Condado, only a block away from the beach. <Author>frostypurplemanatee
<Content>Nice Hotel, Questionable Location The Coral Princess was clean and attractive. The pool is small but appealing and the hot tub was great. We were there during the low tourism season, so often we were the only ones using the tub and pool. The continental breakfast was nice, and the staff was friendly and accommodating. The hotel is only about a $15 cab ride to and from the airport and about $10 to the cruise pier.The downfall of this hotel is the fact the it is surrounded by pretty dumpy places next door and across the street. In fact, I was concerned about going outside after dark the first night we were there. Even though we did venture out after dark subsequently, I still felt insecure once we got off the main drag (Condado) which is about 4 blocks away. This is not the fault of the hotel obviously, but it is something to consider if you are picky about the neighborhood where you stay.We were there 3 nights, and I would not want to stay there longer than that. We probably will not return to PR, but if we did I would not stay in this hotel again because of the condition of the surrounding buildings/area.I highly reccomend other hotels on the main strip because the area is much nicer.Also, the beach was beautiful. It was about 4 blocks away. However, no swimming is permitted because of heavy seas and sharp rocky terrain. If you are a beach person, I would double check to see if you can stay at a hotel with beach access.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Not the best! After reading all the great reviews I decided to stay four nights at the Coral Princess Inn. Staff was helpful but pool was very small. Breakfast was OK nothing to rave about. Beach was a couple of blocks away and the local students drink and party during the day so there was no relaxation time. You can rent chairs and umbrellas for $3.00. The bus ride into San Juan is .25 cents but you often have to wait 45 minutes to an hour or more. Basically if I did not pay upfront I would have stayed at a better location. <Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Excellent - I can't recommend this enough! This is an excellent place to stay for the beach at Condado and local restaurants, shops and bars (a 3 minute walk). Rooms are spotlessly clean, with air conditioning - the inn also has a small pool and a jacuzzi, washing machine facilities and TV and internet access in every room. A buffet breakfast is available from 6-10 (coffee, juice, croissants, ham, cheese, fruit etc). Travel to Old San Juan is easy (the bus stop for the B21 is right around the corner) - although beware - the B21 is infrequent and the last bus leaves San Juan at 9pm. It costs 25 cents one-way so it's worth using if it arrives - a cab into Old San Juan is a 10 minute ride for $8-10.This inn has all the advantages of a small hotel - secure, quiet, well maintained, with a personal service. If you want a hotel with a bar, room service, casino etc - this certainly isn't for you.Our stay here for 6 days was excellent and we certainly plan to return.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Small clean friendly  Just returned from a cruise which started  ended in San Juan  used the Coral Princess as our base before  after.Excellent small  friendly hotel. I tried it after reading so many positive reviews on this site  I was not disappointed!We were lucky enough to have the top floor suite as an upgrade on the first night (before the cruise) and took full advantage of the roof terrace, indoor  outdoor jacquzzis, and a pool table in the living room. Great!On our return we had a standard room but found you can still use the terrace, tubs  pool table...and you have a whirlpool bath in every room anyway!.The breakfast buffet (continental style) was a treat in the lovely airy covered patio on the ground floor, with a good selection of cereals, juice,ham cheese pastries etc.And there's a small but clean  level swimming pool with no deep end, so great if you are a nervous swimmer.Just one downside...the taxi fare to the port cost us around $15-$20 each way, even though it's not that far. So a portside hotel, may be more expensive but at least you would be on site for the cruise. But if you just want to get into Old Town San Juan (which is beautiful) then take the frequent quick  clean buses....it's just 25cents per person!!

<Author>fireblade600
<Content>Safe Haven We stayed here for one night on a forced layover on our way from the US to BVI on our honeymoon. The front desk was very polite, informative, helpful, courteous, and trustworthy. My wife actually forgot her wallet on the chair in the lobby and they held it until we came back through the lobby. The hotel was locked at all times so not just anyone can come in and they know immediately who you are, your name, and you're best interest. The rooms were average to small but clean. The beach is 2 blocks away but i was cautioned that it might not be the safest place. The water was rough and the beach was 'busy' with tourist, locals, vendors, and in my opinion not very relaxing, but we obviously weren't there for the beach anyway. It didn't seem to me like there was much around to see or do otherwise. We took a bus to old san juan which was about a good 40 minute ride during 'happy hour'. We lucked out b/c there was a festival there which was alot of fun. The local buses are dirt cheap and pick up / stop a block away from the coral princess (near the pharmacy which i believe is open 24hrs). Taking a taxi could cost you a fortune and renting a car is a complete waste of money b/c you will literally get run off the road if you try to drive against those locals. I'm not kidding when i say they drive on the sidewalks and they drive full throttle / full horn. Even riding on the bus was like being in a scene from the movie 'Speed'. If you're looking for a fancy hotel or a quaint little BB this boutique hotel is neither. Rather, I think of this place as a 'safe haven' when traveling. I would go back there again b/c it's relatively close to the airport (20 minute taxi ride which the hotel arranges for you), fairly priced, and feels safe, however i would also like to try el Convento which consistently gets good reviews or somewhere in Old San Juan (b/c there's more to walk around and see, shop, dine, etc).  
<Date>May 4, 2005

<Author>Perki
<Content>Nice little hideaway My husband  I stayed one night at this wonderful inn, prior to a cruise. We found the people at the front desk to be very helpful. Our plane landed at 7:00pm and it was just about 7:30pm when we checked in and we were hungry. The lady behind the desk gave us several choices of places all just a block away and of course told us where the Wal-greens was as we forgot a couple of items and needed to get a lighter since they now won't allow them on airplanes. We had Room #17 with a King bed and cost us $165 all taxes, etc included, I think it was $135/$145 or something like that before taxes. Room was very clean, bed was confortable and had plenty to choose from on the TV. I took a shower that night so I could sleep in a little the next morning and not sure if everyone was showering to go out to dinner or what but the temperature of the water kept going from very hot to cold to perfectly warm so I had to keep moving in and out of the water - water pressure was great though. The next morning my husband took a shower and he didn't have this problem so not sure what the reason was that it acted this way with me but just thought I'd mention it as an FYI.At checkout there was another couple ahead of who were disputing phone charges that came up on their bill, they even occured prior to them checking into the hotel so knew they were incorrect. Management credited them so they didn't have to pay and then when we got our bill the same thing happened! Of course we didn't have to pay either but make sure you look at your final bill just in case.Even with these little items I would stay here again in a heartbeat - the character of the building, common areas and rooms was wonderful, you can stay at a cookie cutter hotel anywhere, we wanted something more of a local feel and I would say this has it. Enjoy!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Wonderful Outdoor Facilities I just got back from an 8 days stay at the Coral Princess Inn with my husband and 9 months old baby. We liked the hotel a lot, especially the outdoor facilities (seating area in front of our room and sundeck with jacuzzi!). The rooms + bathrooms are clean and well maintained and ours had a microwave and a fridge (which cannot be missed when vacationing with a baby). Also, the breakfast area / patio is lovely with all the plants and flowers. I had asked for an infant crib when I made the reservation but uppon arrival it turned out to be broken. After calling the front desk about it however, the hotel owner went out to buy a new crib (at 9.30 pm) which was installed for us within the hour. The staff was helpful and nice. The only suggestions to the management would be more closet space and a bit more variety in the breakfast (but its free so what can I say...) I would certainly recommend this hotel if you like a small, layed back, bedbreakfast like accomodation.

<Author>iramcynyc
<Content>Verify your check out time! The hotel itself is clean, pleasant and close to a lovely beach, restaurants and shops. However, we had three complaints.Firstly, unlike the other hotels where we stayed in Puerto Rico (Coral Princess was the third one after a few weeks of traveling throughout the island), there was no bathroom/shower facility to use after the beach once we had checked out. It was our last day and we wanted to go for one last dip in the sea after we had checked out but could not do so since they did not have this amenity. Typically hotels near beaches have this facility, so were a bit surprised. Secondly, parking is impossible to find, so the hotel will direct you to a private parking lot service up the street where you have to pay ten dollars to park per day. The money was not an issue, but unloading and loading the suitcases before moving the cars was (two cars and six girls - a lot of luggage!).And lastly, we were given a printed confirmation before we even got there that our check-out time was at noon. We planned our day accordingly only to be told at the last minute that we had to check out at eleven, which led to an unpleasant argument with the front-desk staff and a scramble to collect our things after breakfast. Overall I would say that after the other hotels we had experienced in Puerto Rico, the Coral Princess was not impressive. But it is definitely less expensive, and if you know what to expect in advance regarding parking, showers and check-out times, it should work out well.

<Author>McC60
<Content>Very quaint, but small rooms We just returned from a stay at the Coral Princess (Mar 21-24,'05). We really liked the place - cute, quaint, nice dipping pool, lovely gardens and very nice staff. Our room was very small, but ok for just a few nights. This is a great location to bus (that goes to Old SJ for .25), restaurants, etc. There is a Wal-Greens just around the corner for those forgotten items. We felt very comfortable walking the around even at 10-11pm. They serve a continental breakfast that is just ok. Not much to choose from and the very same every morning! For the price, $176/nt (we got shafted due to spring break), we probably would not stay there again. All in all, it was fine and it really is in a great location - the larger hotels around that area were about $100 more.

<Content>Great hosts....A wonderful experience My family (wife, and children 8 and 11 year old) and I stayed at the Coral Princess located in Condado 2/19 and 2/20, Washington's Birthday weekend, prior to our cruise. We waited till the last minute and were scrambling a week before to find a place to stay. Nothing was available, no Marriott, no Wyndham, nothing. After looking on line at what was available (not very appealing) , I tried calling some of the highly rated smaller hotels and asking for vacancy or advice where to stay. Two calls led me to the Coral Princess. The only vacancy they had was the penthouse, which cost less than a room at the Marriott a block away. Right upon our arrival we were thrilled. We loved the rooftop hot tub. We loved the kitchen and dining area (we were so tired the first night, we brought back take out) The hotel was very clean!! The marble floor tiles in the room were a nice touch. We loved the continental breakfast on the downstairs patio. The hotel staff was so friendly. The hotel location was excellent, very close to many restaurants and the beach. The hotel staff go out of their way to make your stay special. They even allowed us to store our bags with them after checkout so we could walk around and enjoy the day before we went to the cruise ship.On Saturday night were looking for a restaurant. Ellen, who I think was the manager, must have spent a half hour calling various restaurants trying to get us a table. Being Washington's Birthday weekend it was tough finding getting a reservation. The restaurant she booked us at was outstanding.I looked at a lot of hotel reviews for San Juan hotels on line. There seems to be a prevailing issue with cleanliness/shabbiness/quality. That is not a problem at the Coral Princess!!

<Content>We were very impressed My husband and I just returned from spending a few days in San Juan. We booked the Coral Princess based on reviews found on this website and we were very impressed. Living in the Caribbean we travel to San Juan quite a bit and have stayed at many hotels and this one was a pleasant surprise. We found the staff to be very helpful and the rooms were impeccably clean and tended to promptly each day. The continental breakfast, each morning, was very nice and a good time to mingle with other guests. I thought the price was very reasonable considering it is the high season and also the location, which is right in the center of Condado. This part of the world is very pricey, so if you are looking for a bargain, I think this is definitely it. Everyone and every place has an off day and that has to be considered. However, I can honestly say, we only experienced great things at this hotel and hopefully we will continue to stay there for many trips to come.p.s. there are mini-bars in the rooms with the cheapest prices I've ever seen!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Striving to be the best and it is!!! My wife and I stayed at the Coral Princess Inn on Feb 25th and 26th, 2005 as well as March 6th. We were taking a cruise and knowing the potential for snow in New England, we decided to arrive two days early. As luck would have it, snow arrived on the morning of our departure. I was able to contact the hotel to let them know of our delay in arrival and they were more than accomodating in assuring us that the desk is available 24/7 to check us in since our flight to San Juan would not arrive until after midnight. Upon arrival, we were told that the guest in our room had a medical emergency and we had been upgraded to the penthouse suite. Our rating of this hotel is not because of this upgrade but instead because of the excellent customer service afforded us during our stay and the spotless and tidy cleanliness of the rooms. My wife had suffered a sprained ankle prior to arriving in San Juan and during our first morning at the Coral Princess Inn, the front desk called and wanted to know if they could run out and get us anything that we needed especially room service.(there is no restaurant at the hotel) In addition, I came down with a sinus infection that same day which caused me great discomfort. Not only did they consider this important but they recommended that I go to the hospital emergency room, called us a cab, and promised to hold our checkout procedure as long as possible. As it turned out, we were back before 11:00 am and in time for our regular departure. And finally, I had bought some beer that I was unable take on the cruise with me but they were kind enough to hold it until my return in one week. It sure tasted good as we waited for our room to be ready on March 6th. Without question, this hotel ranks as the best hotel we have ever stayed at in our many excursions because of their continued effort to put customer service ahead of anything else. San Juan is home to many cruise ships, so book early and stay late--You will not be disappointed.

<Author>MBSNJ
<Content>A Really Pretty Place to Stay My husband and I just spent a week at the Coral Princess. It's not a luxury hotel, but it is lovely, with more of the feel of a guesthouse than a hotel. The rooms and public areas are classy - nicely decorated rooms and outdoor public areas with beautiful ceramic tile and lush greenery. Everybody there we came in contact with was friendly and helpful when required, most especially the manager, who gave us advice and then asked follow-up questions to find out how it went.We stayed in the handicap room because it was the only one available with a kitchenette, which we needed because we had to bring our own food for lunch and dinner. It, as well as the room, is small, but we managed OK. There was sometimes a musty smell in the room, which dissipated when we turned up the air conditioner, and the hot water took a very long time to heat up (but once it did it was fine). The bathroom has the feel of a commercial bathroom, which I didn't like because it wasn't pretty, but logically it's appropriate for the room. The upside was that the room is right on the ground floor with the beautiful outdoor courtyard and breakfast area right outside. This was great because even though there is a small table in the room that we could have eaten at, instead we were easily able to take our food right outside and eat at the tables set up for the breakfast. The continental breakfast they served was fine. The neighborhood is great. There are a lot of things for tourists, but it is also somewhat residential and not tacky at all. It also felt very safe. The Walgreen's around the corner was great to have, because it is open 24 hrs. and sold just about everything you could imagine except fresh fruit, which I found in a grocery story down Ashford Ave. The beach is very close by, and is the same beach that the Marriot Hotel opens onto. It is very clean and beautiful, and you could rent lounge chairs right there for $3.00/day. We rented a car and it was very easy to get to the highway from the hotel. The parking was not a problem - in addition to the 4 hotel spots and the backup parking for $10 down the block, there was street parking, which we were able to find right across the street. I would definitely recommend Puerto Rico, the Condado neighborhood, and the Coral Princess.  
<Date>Feb 27, 2005

<Content>Great hotel for the price My wife and I stayed at this hotel for one night before a cruise of Feb. 11, 2005. The hotel was very clean and the staff were friendly and helpful. <Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great Value My girlfriend and I just got back from a 5 day stay at the Coral Princess and loved it. We stayed in the penthouse (3rd floor). The room was big (only two penthouse rooms on the 3rd floor) and cleanly kept by the staff. The room has a small balcony leading onto a roof patio with a small jacuzzi. The hotel is 1/2 block from Walgreens and two blocks from the beach. A nice Argentinian restaurant is locked within 100 feet of the hotel. The staff was friendly and very helpful in recommending bars  restaurants. This hotel is a great value if you are looking for something that cost less than the chain hotels located just a few blocks away (the Marriott is about 1 1/2 blocks). The continental breakfast was nice but nothing special....that's about the worst thing I can say about the Coral Princess. I would definitely stay there again.Also, we highly recommend taking the rainforest tour. We toured with Sunshine Tours. The guide's name was Rupert. He was very knowledgeable, a gentleman and a great conversationalist. After touring the rainforest we stopped by Loquilla beach which was okay but nothing special. The rainforest is a must, Loquilla beach is not.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great hotel for the money!! We stayed at the Coral Princess 1/29-2/3 and loved it. We stayed on the Penthouse (3rd floor) level and pretty much had the whole space to ourselves. It has a beautifully decorated common area with couches, tables, full kitchen, pool table and a wonderful rooftop deck with a great little jacuzzi.The staff were extremely friendly and helpful, the continental breakfast was nicely done. The entire hotel is very well kept and sweet. We were close to the beach, Walgreen's and all the good restaurants, three blocks from Avis, where we rented a car several days, and a short cab ride from Old San Juan.We recommend Cieto Lindo, a very yummy  affordable Mexican restaurant just a block from the hotel on Magdalena. Be careful driving in Puerto Rico. The road signs are horrible and the drivers are worse. There are no rules in Puerto Rico!!! I recommend you buy a good road map at a book store, prior to your trip, if you plan on doing any driving.Other than that, we had an amazing time, and this hotel is the perfect resting place.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Recommended hotel but with some recommendations to the staff Last January 4th I stayed at this charming hotel. The hotel is hip and in and excellent location. Compared to other hotels in the Condado area, this one is one of the most updated, clean and well kept. The staff needs to get a little bit of training on hospitality. Upon our arrival the guy in the front left us waiting for about 20 minutes and there was nobody else we could speak to for checking in. Also, the cart of the cleaning lady was in the lobby and when we tried to move it so that we could go accross the lobby the lady yelled at us and the guy on the front desk didn't apologize on her behalf. Parking is limitted. Another recommendation will be that for such beautiful decor the bed covers should be all white as well as the sheets on the beds. The current linens don't match the sophistication and style that the hotel wants to portray. The breakfast in the morning(which was included on the price) was absolutely great and well presented. The breakfast area was relaxing and absolutely gorgeous full of orchids and tropical plants. Even though I make these suggestions to the management of the hotel I will rate the hotel like one of the best kept secrets in the Condado area, which is well worth the try.

<Author>ChiswickTurnhamGreen
<Content>Recommended My boyfriend and I stayed at the Coral Pincess Inn at the beginning of December. Overall the Inn is great - 9 out of 10. Key facts are: it's spotlessly clean everywhere. With no exceptions, the staff are incredibly nice, friendly and helpful. The place has a funky feel as it has pretty minimal decoration plus some interesting modern art by a local artist (they have her contact details at reception if you want to buy). Everything you need is very local - the local store is the Walgreens half a block away and the beach is 2 blocks away. The Inn serves a cold breakfast that is ok. Drawbacks for the new visitor: The rooms are on the small side but we were hardly there so that was fine with us. All we wanted was a clean, well air conned room with a shower that worked. Which is what you get.There is no pool. (The spa on the roof is ok but the let the whole of the top floor, incuding the spa, on day 3 and so it was out of bounds from then on).We went in December for 6 days. 3 of those days were wet with heavy rain for the majority of the time. The good news is that San Juan has enough to do for when it is rainy (unlike some other Caribbean islands). Also, the other three days were beautiful with strong sunshine and temps in 80s.The beach by the Inn is not your typical Caribbean ideal beach. It on the windward side of the island so this means you get a small bit of sand, a steep drop off, lots and lots of wind and big waves. We loved the waves (they actually made the holiday for us) but if you want tranquil, blue and 'all you can hear is waves gently washing the beach' silence go elsewhere or treck to other parts of the island.Gay-wise, the area is cool with gays but the club is 10 mins taxi ride and the (large) gay bar near the Inn (4 blocks away) was dead day and night. December is not obviously not peak gay season!I would definitely stay here if I came to PR again.  
<Date>Jan 9, 2005

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Clean, nice decor, OK rates My new wife and I spent 7 days and nights at the Coral Princess for our Honeymoon in Puerto Rico. The room was always clean, the decor was charming (a mix of traditional Spanish with some local artwork and tasteful modern furniture) and the staff generally helpful. The breakfast was OK; a non-varying assortment of pastries, orange juice, coffee, bananas, wrapped slices of cheese and lunchmeat with croissant bread. The hot tub on the 3rd floor was unavailable for general use, and the one occasion that we did get to use it, it did not work properly anyway. Inexplicably, there was always only one small drinking glass available in the room, but since I never asked for another, I suppose I cannot complain. The shower was OK, but lacked much force in the streams and would frequently cycle between warm and cold for no apparent reason. The price ($110 a night, plus tax, plus an energy surcharge of around $8.00 a day that I was previously unaware of, seemed a little steep for the room size and amenities). The BIG question - would I stay there again? Yes, without a doubt, BUT I would certainly check for bargains from other places. AND one more hint - DO NOT rent a car except for the days you plan to do a lot of driving. Driving and parking are OK at times, major headaches at others. Take the bus, publicos, or a taxi and save money and aggravation. Go see El Yunque and Old San Juan - don't bother going to Ponce unless you are fond of finding your way through labyrinth-style unmarked streets that go only in one direction. All told, our vacation in PR and our stay in the Coral Princess were very memorable. Hope your vacation is wonderful.  
<Date>Dec 17, 2004

<Author>Sansonee
<Content>Comfortable and Clean! Stayed one night prior to cruise and the rooms were extremely clean. Marble tile floors kept the room really cold - it was great! Jacuzzi tub looks brand new! Bed was comfortable. Rooms are cozy yet comfortable in size although we didn't spend much time in our room other than to sleep. We didn't have time to use the pool or hot tub but we checked them out and they looked clean. The tropical plants and orchids were a nice touch! Coral Princess is one block from Ashford Ave (near the Marriott Hotel) - convenient to shopping, dining, and public transportation. We took the bus (around the corner near Walgreens) for $.25/person to the last stop in Old San Juan where we picked up the free trolley for our own tour of the City as the hotel staff had advised. Also, the hotel staff allowed us to leave our luggage with them (locked in the office) after we checked out so we could explore the city before we boarded our cruise ship. Hotel staff was very helpful with recommendations for dining as well as arranging a taxi for us. If I ever find myself in Puerto Rico again, I will definitely stay here again without hesitation.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great little place I booked a 4 night stay at the Coral Princess based on the reviews I had read on this website. The hotel was absolutely adorable, the rooms were comfortable and spotless. The staff was very professional and very friendly, and the hotel is situated 2 blocks from the beach and around the corner from a strip of some great restaurants and bars. Breakfast was so-so, and there was a slight musty smell in the room, but all-in-all I would definitely recommend this if you are looking for something affordable in San Juan. For food, I recommend Hermes Oyster Bar - by far the best Mojitos I've ever had (the bartender would not divulge his secret ingredient) - which was about a block from the hotel. La Dorada, which was right around the corner, also had some great Puerto Rican/seafood fare, and came highly recommended by most of the locals. Enjoy!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Wouldn't stay anywhere else in San Juan! Stayed here on business in mid-June 2004. If you are going to visit San Juan you would be cheating yourself if you stay at a big hotel. The Coral Princess Inn allows you to get the native feel of San Juan. The property has been incredibly renovated. The rooms are a decent size (at least mine was), with a refrigerator. The new air conditioners work like a charm! Althought the pool is some what small, the beach is only 2 blocks away. There is a hot tub up on the 3rd floor as well as a pool table and a full kitchen. Surrounded by all kinds of good places to eat. The continential breakfast was very good. Best of all the staff was very friendly and helpful. All the amentities of a big resort, but the piece and quiet of a private cottage. Only problem is parking. They only have 4 spots in front of the hotel. We always were able to get one of the 4, but if not you only have to walk a minute to a parking lot the hotel has a contract with. If you stay here you won't be disspointed.

<Author>patsbosoxfan
<Content>A fabulous find I discovered The Coral Princess through tripadvisor.com. The recommendations are absolutely correct. This was a lovely hotel in the Condado area. We stayed for one night following a cruise and were upgraded to a penthouse because the hotel was not full. This room was incredible! It was spacious with amenities including a jacuzzi tub and weight bench in the room and a private balcony (shared only by the three penthouse rooms) with a hot tub. In addition to this spacious room, the staff amazed us with their willingness to satisfy their guests. We wanted to head to El Yunque. When the front desk was unable to procure a tour, the manager (Luis?) called a friend at a car rental agency. A van immediately picked us up at the front door and brought us to a local car rental company. More astounding was what we discovered at El Yunque. While heading back to our car, we saw the hotel manager. He explained that another couple wanted to see the rain forest and were not able to drive a car. So-he brought them there on a private tour with a one hour drive each way. What incredible service!!!! I strongly recommend this hotel in San Juan!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Had a great stay! My husband and I stayed at the Coral Princess for ten nights in february, 2004. This was our first visit to Puerto Rico, so we were unccertain of what to expect. The Coral Princess was a delightful place to stay! It was a quiet oasis in the middle of a very busy area. We enjoyed the nearby convenience of wonderful local restaurants, a beautiful beach, and nighttime entertainment. We took the local bus into Old San Juan several times - it was an easy way to travel, since we did not rent a car during our stay there.The staff was very friendly and helpful. They booked some excursions for us - even made travel arrangements for us to take the ferry over to the Island of Vieques.My only complaint was that the room was very small. We booked one of their higher priced rooms, expecting much more space. There was no view to speak of from our window. However, the public areas of the inn were very quaint and attractive, so we made good use of these facilities. I would return there again.

<Author>beachbunnee
<Content>Little Piece of Paradise We stayed at the Coral Princess Inn from April 7th to April 13th. It's a little piece of paradise centrally located right amongst the hustle and bustle of the Condado area. The Inn is very well maintained and the live-in management ensured that everything was running smoothly. The entire property was spotlessly clean. We enjoyed the continental breakfast each morning and had the little pool and rooftop hot tub to ourselves every time we used them. Our Executive room with a queen bed was located in a building at the rear of the Inn and it was quiet and private. We had a jacuzzi tub, small frig, and a microwave. It was unfortunate that there was some noisy street excavation going on in front of the Inn, but I guess that is an unpreventable thing that can occur no matter where you stay. There is limited parking on the Inn property, but when that was not available we always got lucky and found a spot nearby on the street for our rental car. The Inn is within easy walking distance to the beach, casinos, and restaurants. The neighborhood appeared safe. We will definitely return to the Coral Princess Inn.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Perfect small retreat within Condado We live in the Virgin Islands and travel to Puerto Rico once or twice a year to get off the rock. We have been looking for a unique, friendly small establishment to stay in as an alternative to the corporate hotels. Boy, did we find it. The rooms were clean and modern - ours had a nice big jacuzzi tub. The outside spaces in the hotel are tiled in Mexican Saltillo tile and filled with palms, bougainvillea, and many varieties of orchids that some enterprising green thumb has gone to great lengths to cultivate. We very much enjoyed the sun deck on the roof with the jacuzzi - it was the perfect place to escape the hustle bustle of Condado and read a book. Someone has clearly gone to great lengths to create the kind of place they would want to stay - from the full-size modern kitchen and pool table on the third floor to the reading room with chess table on the ground floor, a lot of love has gone into this little place. We will definitely be back.  
<Date>Apr 6, 2004

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Relief! Just got back from a week long trip to Puerto Rico (4/4/2004), and stayed at the Coral Princess for 2 nights right before we left to come back home. Wish that I would have stayed at the Coral Princess for longer! It is a small 20-some room inn in the Condado area, about a 10-15 minute ride from the airport. It has a small swimming pool and a rooftop hot tub, but the beach is only a two block walk (an easy one). The continental breakfast was decent, enough to get you going in the morning, but could be improved. The hotel/room was very clean, and I felt safe there. There is a 24 hour Walgreens right around the corner, and many restaurants (both fast food and sit-down restaurants) and shops in within walking distance. The bus to Old San Juan is a block away and only costs 25 cents compared to taking a taxi for $10. There are some of the big hotels a block away if you want to go to the casino or partake in some of their entertainment. The staff is very friendly at the Coral Princess and very informative as well. I highly recommend you stay here if you want to save a lot of money.  
<Date>Apr 4, 2004
